\DoxyCodeLine{978 \textcolor{comment}{// Generic getInfoHelper. The final parameter is used to guide overload}}
\DoxyCodeLine{979 \textcolor{comment}{// resolution: the actual parameter passed is an int, which makes this}}
\DoxyCodeLine{980 \textcolor{comment}{// a worse conversion sequence than a specialization that declares the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{981 \textcolor{comment}{// parameter as an int.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{982 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Functor, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{983 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(Functor f, cl\_uint name, T* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{long})}
\DoxyCodeLine{984 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{985     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} f(name, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T), param, NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{986 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{987 }
\DoxyCodeLine{988 \textcolor{comment}{// Specialized for getInfo<CL\_PROGRAM\_BINARIES>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{989 \textcolor{comment}{// Assumes that the output vector was correctly resized on the way in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{990 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func>}
\DoxyCodeLine{991 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(Func f, cl\_uint name, vector<vector<unsigned char>>* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int})}
\DoxyCodeLine{992 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{993     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (name != CL\_PROGRAM\_BINARIES) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{994         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_INVALID\_VALUE;}
\DoxyCodeLine{995     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{996     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (param) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{997         \textcolor{comment}{// Create array of pointers, calculate total size and pass pointer array in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{998         size\_type numBinaries = param-\/>size();}
\DoxyCodeLine{999         vector<unsigned char*> binariesPointers(numBinaries);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1000 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1001         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (size\_type i = 0; i < numBinaries; ++i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1002         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1003             binariesPointers[i] = (*param)[i].data();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1004         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1005 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1006         cl\_int err = f(name, numBinaries * \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char}*), binariesPointers.data(), NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1007 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1008         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1009             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1010         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1011     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1012 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1013 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1014     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1015 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1016 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1017 \textcolor{comment}{// Specialized getInfoHelper for vector params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1018 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1019 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(Func f, cl\_uint name, vector<T>* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{long})}
\DoxyCodeLine{1020 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1021     size\_type required;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1022     cl\_int err = f(name, 0, NULL, \&required);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1023     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1024         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1025     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1026     \textcolor{keyword}{const} size\_type elements = required / \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(T);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1027 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1028     \textcolor{comment}{// Temporary to avoid changing param on an error}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1029     vector<T> localData(elements);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1030     err = f(name, required, localData.data(), NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1031     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1032         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1033     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1034     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (param) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1035         *param = std::move(localData);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1036     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1037 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1038     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1039 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1040 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1041 \textcolor{comment}{/* Specialization for reference-\/counted types. This depends on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1042 \textcolor{comment}{ * existence of Wrapper<T>::cl\_type, and none of the other types having the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1043 \textcolor{comment}{ * cl\_type member. Note that simplify specifying the parameter as Wrapper<T>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1044 \textcolor{comment}{ * does not work, because when using a derived type (e.g. Context) the generic}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1045 \textcolor{comment}{ * template will provide a better match.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1046 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1047 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1048 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(}
\DoxyCodeLine{1049     Func f, cl\_uint name, vector<T>* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T::cl\_type = 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1050 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1051     size\_type required;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1052     cl\_int err = f(name, 0, NULL, \&required);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1053     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1054         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1055     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1056 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1057     \textcolor{keyword}{const} size\_type elements = required / \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T::cl\_type);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1058 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1059     vector<typename T::cl\_type> value(elements);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1060     err = f(name, required, value.data(), NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1061     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1062         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1063     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1064 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1065     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (param) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1066         \textcolor{comment}{// Assign to convert CL type to T for each element}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1067         param-\/>resize(elements);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1068 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1069         \textcolor{comment}{// Assign to param, constructing with retain behaviour}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1070         \textcolor{comment}{// to correctly capture each underlying CL object}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1071         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (size\_type i = 0; i < elements; i++) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1072             (*param)[i] = T(value[i], \textcolor{keyword}{true});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1073         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1074     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1075     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1076 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1077 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1078 \textcolor{comment}{// Specialized GetInfoHelper for string params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1079 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func>}

\DoxyCodeLine{1081 \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1087 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1088     \textcolor{comment}{// std::string has a constant data member}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1089     \textcolor{comment}{// a char vector does not}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1090     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (required > 0) \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{1092         err = f(name, required, value.data(), NULL);}

\DoxyCodeLine{1095         \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1097             param-\/>assign(begin(value), prev(end(value)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{1098         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1099     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1100     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (param) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1101         param-\/>assign(\textcolor{stringliteral}{"{}"{}});}
\DoxyCodeLine{1102     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1103     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1104 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1106 \textcolor{comment}{// Specialized GetInfoHelper for clsize\_t params}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1107 \textcolor{keyword}{template} <\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func, \textcolor{keywordtype}{size\_t}ype N>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1108 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(Func f, cl\_uint name, array<size\_type, N>* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{long})}
\DoxyCodeLine{1109 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1110     size\_type required;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1111     cl\_int err = f(name, 0, NULL, \&required);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1112     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1113         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1114     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1115 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1116     size\_type elements = required / \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(size\_type);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1117     vector<size\_type> value(elements, 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1118 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1119     err = f(name, required, value.data(), NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1120     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1121         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1122     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1123     }
\DoxyCodeLine{1124     \textcolor{comment}{// Bound the copy with N to prevent overruns}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1125     \textcolor{comment}{// if passed N > than the amount copied}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1126     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (elements > N) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1127         elements = N;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1128     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1129     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (size\_type i = 0; i < elements; ++i) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1130         (*param)[i] = value[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{1131     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1132 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1133     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1134 \}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1136 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} T> \textcolor{keyword}{struct }ReferenceHandler;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1137 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1138 \textcolor{comment}{/* Specialization for reference-\/counted types. This depends on the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1139 \textcolor{comment}{ * existence of Wrapper<T>::cl\_type, and none of the other types having the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1140 \textcolor{comment}{ * cl\_type member. Note that simplify specifying the parameter as Wrapper<T>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1141 \textcolor{comment}{ * does not work, because when using a derived type (e.g. Context) the generic}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1143 \textcolor{comment}{ */}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1144 \textcolor{keyword}{template}<\textcolor{keyword}{typename} Func, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T>}
\DoxyCodeLine{1145 \textcolor{keyword}{inline} cl\_int getInfoHelper(Func f, cl\_uint name, T* param, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}, \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T::cl\_type = 0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1146 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1147     \textcolor{keyword}{typename} T::cl\_type value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1148     cl\_int err = f(name, \textcolor{keyword}{sizeof}(value), \&value, NULL);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1149     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1150         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1151     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1152     *param = value;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1153     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (value != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1154     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1155         err = param-\/>retain();}
\DoxyCodeLine{1156         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (err != CL\_SUCCESS) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1157             \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} err;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1158         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1159     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1160     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} CL\_SUCCESS;}

\DoxyCodeLine{1746 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if CL\_HPP\_TARGET\_OPENCL\_VERSION >= 120 \&\& CL\_HPP\_MINIMUM\_OPENCL\_VERSION < 120}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1747 \textcolor{comment}{// Extracts version number with major in the upper 16 bits, minor in the lower 16}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1748 \textcolor{keyword}{static} cl\_uint getVersion(\textcolor{keyword}{const} vector<char> \&versionInfo)}
\DoxyCodeLine{1749 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1750     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} highVersion = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1751     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} lowVersion = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1752     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} index = 7;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1753     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(versionInfo[index] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'.'} ) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1754         highVersion *= 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1755         highVersion += versionInfo[index]-\/\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1756         ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1757     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1758     ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1759     \textcolor{keywordflow}{while}(versionInfo[index] != \textcolor{charliteral}{' '} \&\&  versionInfo[index] != \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1760         lowVersion *= 10;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1761         lowVersion += versionInfo[index]-\/\textcolor{charliteral}{'0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{1762         ++index;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1763     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1764     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} (highVersion << 16) | lowVersion;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1765 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1766 }

\DoxyCodeLine{1768 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{1769     size\_type size = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{1770     clGetPlatformInfo(platform, CL\_PLATFORM\_VERSION, 0, NULL, \&size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1771 }
\DoxyCodeLine{1772     vector<char> versionInfo(size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1773     clGetPlatformInfo(platform, CL\_PLATFORM\_VERSION, size, versionInfo.data(), \&size);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1774     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} getVersion(versionInfo);}
\DoxyCodeLine{1775 \}}
